on_institution_embracement = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_attribute = monarch_power_on_institutions
		}
		add_adm_power = 100
		add_dip_power = 100
		add_mil_power = 100
	}
	if = { #Artificery start general
		limit = {
			has_institution = manufactories
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = artificery_unlocked
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { religion = bulwari_sun_cult }
				is_chosen_country = no
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = anbennar_setup.19
		}
	}
	if = { #Anbennar - isobelin events
		limit = {
			tag = G91
			has_institution = global_trade
		}
		country_event = { 
			id = flavor_isobelin.10 #goblin cartels
			days = 3650
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = G43 
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = haraf_has_reformed_kinah
			}
			2112 = {
                has_active_triggered_province_modifier = haraf_finished_integration
            }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = haraf_events.8
		}
		add_stability = -2
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = R03 } has_institution = manufactories }
		country_event = { id = sanghariyar.7 days = 3650 }
	}
}

on_national_focus_change = {}

#ROOT = new capital province, FROM = old capital province
on_capital_moved = {
	on_capital_moved_effect = yes
	# if your capital is moved to a colony (i.e. by losing all your other provinces)
	# this colony auto-completes to a province without triggering on_colony_finished
	# so catch this edge case here to fix the pop modifiers
	# stupidly, when it triggers this on_action it's both a colony and your capital
	if = {
		limit = { is_colony = yes }
		province_event = { id = race_setup_events.15 }
	}


	if = { limit = { has_province_modifier = cant_colonize }	#Anbennar
		province_event = { id = migration_force_settle.3 days = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		#Not Anbennar
		if = { #removes/sets dev cost bonus on capital state for government reforms
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_government_attribute = lower_dev_cost_in_capital_state
				}
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = lower_dev_cost_in_capital_state_modifier }
			}
			FROM = {
				area = {
					remove_province_modifier = lower_dev_cost_in_capital_state_modifier
				}
			}
			area = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = lower_dev_cost_in_capital_state_modifier
					duration = -1
					hidden = yes
				}
			}
		}
	
		#Anbennar
		if = { #removes/sets gov cost bonus on capital region for government reforms
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_government_attribute = lower_gov_cost_in_home_region
				}
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = lower_gov_cost_in_home_region_modifier }
			}
			FROM = {
				region = {
					remove_province_modifier = lower_gov_cost_in_home_region_modifier
				}
			}
			area = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = lower_gov_cost_in_home_region_modifier
					duration = -1
					hidden = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	owner = {	
		country_event = { id = escanni_wars.3 } # Escanni wars bypass
		country_event = { id = escanni_wars.200 } # Joined Escanni wars
		country_event = { id = flavour_splinter.2 } # Itinerant Capital
	}
	
	#update "Religion Triumphant" HRE modifiers
	owner = { country_event = { id = religious_leagues.11 } }
	
	#dwarovar reclaimer
	if = { limit = { continent = serpentspine }
		owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = reclaiming_dwarovar duration = -1 } }
	}
	else = {
		owner = { remove_country_modifier = reclaiming_dwarovar }
	}

	FROM = { #Close hold digging gui on old capital
		clr_province_flag = diggy_diggy_estimate_flag
	}

	# move "arcane battery capital complex" invention
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arcane_battery_capital_complex
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			remove_province_modifier = artifice_arcane_battery_capital_complex
		}
		ROOT = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = artifice_arcane_battery_capital_complex
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	
	yrw_move_iosahar_debug_modifier = yes
	#CENTAUR NOMADISM
	
	if = {
		limit = {
				owner = {
					has_government_attribute = centaur_nomadism_attribute
				}
		}
		ROOT = {	
			owner = {
				save_event_target_as = the_centaur_who_moved
				add_country_modifier = {
						name = nomadic_capital_just_moved
						duration = 1825
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_province_flag = is_nomadic_capital
						}
					}
					clr_province_flag = is_nomadic_capital
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = centaur_free_temple
						capital_scope = {
							NOT = { has_building = temple }
						}
					}
					capital_scope = {
						add_building_construction = {
							building = temple
							cost = 0
						}
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government_attribute = centaur_COT_free_development
					}
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
								has_province_modifier = centaur_COT_capital	
						}
						remove_province_modifier = centaur_COT_capital
					}
					capital_scope = {
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = centaur_COT_capital
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			owner = {
				apply_debuff_NZOC_country_scope = yes
				apply_owned_NZOC_country = yes
			}	
		}
	}

	#Irkorzik itinerant capital
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				AND = {
					has_reform = irkorzik_dunesworn_council_reform
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			owner = {
				capital_scope = { set_province_flag = F69_capital_counter }
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				AND = {
					has_reform = irkorzik_dunesworn_council_reform
					has_country_flag = irkorzik_itinerant_capital
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			owner = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_capital }
					remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_capital
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = irkorzik_capital_moved
					duration = 1825
				}
				capital_scope = { 
					every_province_in_state = { 
						add_permanent_province_modifier = {
							name = irkorzik_capital
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				AND = {
					has_reform = irkorzik_dunesworn_council_reform
					has_country_flag = irkorzik_itinerant_capital_bonus_church_power
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			owner = {
				add_church_power = 40
			}
		}
	}
}

#ROOT = province that was expanded in, FROM = country that did it
on_expanded_infrastructure = {
	# Ovdal Tngr Improved Trading Post system.
	if = { limit = { FROM = { tag = F23 has_reform = F23_the_port_hold } OR = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 has_river_estuary_trigger = yes } }
		F23_apply_improved_trading_post = yes
	}
	owner = { accretive_path_generic_chi_stacking_effect = { amount = 20 } }
}

#ROOT = province that was centralized in
on_centralized_state = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_government_attribute = centralize_state_no_reform_cost }
		}
		owner = {
			add_adm_power = 50
			change_government_reform_progress = 50
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_government_attribute = centralize_state_half_refund NOT = { has_age_ability = ab_ruinborn_empire } }
		}
		owner = {
			add_adm_power = 25
			change_government_reform_progress = 25
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { 
				OR = {
					has_government_attribute = centralize_state_development
					has_age_ability = ab_ruinborn_empire
				}
			}
		}
		area = {
			limit = {
				owned_by = ROOT
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = { add_base_tax = 1 }
				1 = { add_base_production = 1 }
				1 = { add_base_manpower = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

on_new_age = {
	set_age_passed_global_flag = yes
	remove_all_age_timed_modifiers = yes

	#Consolidation wars events
	events = {
		escanni_wars.1 # Fire the war

#ROOT = province
on_adm_exploited = {
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_government_attribute = may_not_reduce_tax_on_exploitation } }
		random = {
			chance = 50
			add_base_tax = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_government_attribute = may_not_reduce_tax_on_own_exploitation culture_group = ROOT } }
		random = {
			chance = 25
			add_base_tax = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_government_attribute = may_not_reduce_tax_on_foreign_exploitation NOT = { culture_group = ROOT } } }
		random = {
			chance = 50
			add_base_tax = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			owner = { has_government_attribute = centaur_refund_exploit_dev }
			has_province_modifier = base_nomadic_zone_of_control 
		}
		add_base_tax = 1
		add_devastation = 15
	}

	#Ayarellen
	if = { limit = { owner = { tag = F27 } culture = sadnatu } change_variable = { which = f27_sadnatu_development value = -1 } }
	if = { limit = { owner = { tag = F27 } culture = surani } change_variable = { which = f27_surani_development value = -1 } }
	if = { limit = { owner = { tag = F27 } culture = masnsih } change_variable = { which = f27_masnsih_development value = -1 } }
	if = { limit = { owner = { tag = F27 } culture = brasanni } change_variable = { which = f27_brasanni_development value = -1 } }
	if = { limit = { owner = { tag = F27 } culture = zanite } change_variable = { which = f27_zanite_development value = -1 } }
	if = { limit = { owner = { tag = F27 } culture = kuzarami } change_variable = { which = f27_kuzarami_development value = -1 } }
	if = { limit = { owner = { tag = F27 } culture = bahari } change_variable = { which = f27_bahari_development value = -1 } }
	if = { limit = { owner = { tag = F27 } culture = gelkar } change_variable = { which = f27_gelkar_development value = -1 } }
	if = { limit = { owner = { tag = F27 } culture = maqeti } change_variable = { which = f27_maqeti_development value = -1 } }
	if = { limit = { owner = { tag = F27 } culture = sandfang_gnoll } change_variable = { which = f27_sandfang_development value = -1 } }

	#Karakhanbar
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				has_country_flag = karakhanbar_not_losing_development_chance
			}
		}
		random = {
			chance = 50
			add_base_tax = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					religion = summer_court
					religion = winter_court
				}				
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_church_power = -4
		}
	}
}

on_raze = {
	add_permanent_province_modifier = {
		name = province_razed
		duration = 7300
	}
	xhazobkult_terrain_razing = yes
	owner = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = centaur_administration
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = nbProvincesRazed
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {has_government_attribute = scourge_of_irdaeos_reform_raze_effect}
			has_province_modifier = base_nomadic_zone_of_control
		}
		export_to_variable = {
    		which = scourgeDev
    		value = development
    		who = ROOT
		}
		while = {
            limit = {
                #While our total dip value has 1, lower dip power by 1.
                check_variable = {
                    which = scourgeDev
                    value = 1
                }
            }
            owner = {
				add_treasury = 5
			}
            subtract_variable = {
                which = scourgeDev
                value = 1
            }
        }
	}
}

on_concentrate_development = {
	if = { #1.35
		limit = { 
			owner = { has_country_modifier = fra_french_isles_modifier }
		}
		add_nationalism = -5
	}
}

# EVERYTHING BELOW 1.35
on_slacken_start = {
    if = { #no slacken pls
        limit = {
			has_country_modifier = shadow_pact_madness_mod
        }
        add_army_professionalism = 0.01
    }
    else = {
        add_country_modifier = {
            name = slackening_modifier
            duration = -1
        }
    }
}
on_slacken_stop = {
	remove_country_modifier = slackening_modifier
}

on_colony_finished = { #ROOT - Province
	events = {
		kheionai.99 #Fires the nekhei province transfer effects so the game doesn't crash
		gerudia.35 #Taric and Cagodic stuff
	}
	on_colony_finished_effect = yes

	# Anbennar
	province_event = { id = race_setup_events.15 }	
	# colonies do not get their pops updated to match the owners (even though the culture is the owners primary)
	# until the colony is complete

	g27_breluslad_supplies_effect = yes
	g27_breluslad_village_elections_effect = yes
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_monstrous_tribes_promise_new_lands } }
		owner = { change_estate_land_share = { estate = estate_monstrous_tribes share = 1 } }
	}

	#Beggaston
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				has_country_modifier = beggaston_sarda_pioneers
			}
			region = veykoda_region
		}
		change_culture = sarda
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = U08_cleared_coast }
			area = coastal_krahway_area
		}
		ROOT = {
		remove_province_modifier = ekha_coastal_krahway_cleared
		}
	}
}

on_core = { #ROOT - Province, #FROM - Country that gets the core
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { OR = { religion = gods_of_the_taychend religion = oren_nayiru } } }
		FROM = { gain_taychend_glory_effect = { amount = 10 } }
	}

	#Restoring upgrades if an order was deactivated but not destroyed due to the state only being partially conquered (and you losing the core in the meantime)
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = upgraded_balgar }
			holy_order = balgar_order
			area_for_scope_province  = {
				type = all
				owner = {
					ROOT = { owned_by = PREV }
					is_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		area = {
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = corinite_balgar_upgraded
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = upgraded_corin }
			holy_order = corin_order
			area_for_scope_province  = {
				type = all
				owner = {
					ROOT = { owned_by = PREV }
					is_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		area = {
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = corinite_corin_upgraded
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = upgraded_falah }
			holy_order = falah_order
			area_for_scope_province  = {
				type = all
				owner = {
					ROOT = { owned_by = PREV }
					is_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		area = {
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = corinite_falah_upgraded
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = upgraded_munas }
			holy_order = munas_order
			area_for_scope_province  = {
				type = all
				owner = {
					ROOT = { owned_by = PREV }
					is_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		area = {
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = corinite_munas_upgraded
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = upgraded_ryala }
			holy_order = ryala_order
			area_for_scope_province  = {
				type = all
				owner = {
					ROOT = { owned_by = PREV }
					is_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		area = {
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = corinite_ryala_upgraded
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

on_scorch_earth = { #ROOT - scorching country, FROM - scorched province
	FROM = {
		on_scorch_earth_effect = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { 
				has_country_flag = karakhanbar_powerful_scorch_earth
				has_wartaxes = yes
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			every_neighbor_province = {
				limit = {
					controlled_by = ROOT
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = scorched_earth }
				}
				add_devastation = 10
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = scorched_earth
					duration = 1825
				}
				on_scorch_earth_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
	ROOT = { accretive_path_beikling_chi_stacking_effect = { amount = 5 } }
}

		}
	}
	FROM = { 
		country_event = { id = ashtreepact.2 } 
		every_ally = {
			limit = { religion = ashentree_pact }
			country_event = { id = ashtreepact.2 }
		}
	}

	#Khao Elnak War Counter - remove the control flag
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = Y62
			has_country_flag = khao_at_war
		}
		clr_country_flag = khao_at_war
	}
}

on_alliance_created = { #ROOT - Alliance sender, FROM - Alliance accepter
	If = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = A75_alenic_blood_flag
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = A75_alenic_blood
			}
			FROM = {
				tag = A30
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = A75_alenic_blood
			duration = -1
			desc = UNTIL_ALLIANCE_BROKEN
		}
		FROM = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = A75_alenic_blood
				duration = -1
				desc = UNTIL_ALLIANCE_BROKEN
			}
		}
	}
}

on_royal_marriage = { #ROOT - Marraige sender, FROM - marriage accepter
}

on_heir_disinherited = {
	if = {
		limit = { 
			has_ruler_modifier = heir_mage_personality_mod 
		}
		remove_country_modifier = heir_mage_personality_mod
	}
}		
on_overrun = { #ROOT - winner, FROM - loser, on stackwipe
}
